{\footnotesize template$<$typename V, typename Enabled = bool\+\_\+constant$<$b\+Unique\+Keys$>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{hashtable_8h_a7208b11ab4342444a2643d96c0add8c7}{ENABLE\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+TRUETYPE}}(Enabled) = nullptr$>$ }\\\mbox{\hyperlink{structeastl_1_1pair}{eastl\+::pair}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_ab8c71d59d872293db64a74ce62e5c1ae}{iterator}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_a93b1c76ffdd3763db27bae2088415d91}{Do\+Insert\+Value\+Extra\+Forwarding}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_ab71d9359ab4dbf7b609d9f5680e28843}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_a1eaece963a5369fae833f9602edc11d4}{key\+\_\+type}} \&k, \mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_a1cb09e7d5d957f512e22dfbe44644c0f}{hash\+\_\+code\+\_\+t}} c, \mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_a425582405b9c6febecfe09cd9c829db0}{node\+\_\+type}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}p\+Node\+New, V \&\&\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a1b2be7bfa84f129a2690a62f3ad82d62}{value}})

\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Key, typename Value, typename Allocator, typename Extract\+Key, typename Equal, typename H1, typename H2, typename H, typename Rehash\+Policy, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} b\+Cache\+Hash\+Code, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} b\+Mutable\+Iterators, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} b\+Unique\+Keys$>$\newline
class eastl\+::hashtable$<$ Key, Value, Allocator, Extract\+Key, Equal, H1, H2, H, Rehash\+Policy, b\+Cache\+Hash\+Code, b\+Mutable\+Iterators, b\+Unique\+Keys $>$}
hashtable

Key and Value\+: arbitrary Copy\+Constructible types.

Extract\+Key\+: function object that takes a object of type Value and returns a value of type Key.

Equal\+: function object that takes two objects of type k and returns a bool-\/like value that is true if the two objects are considered equal.

H1\+: a hash function. A unary function object with argument type Key and result type size\+\_\+t. Return values should be distributed over the entire range \mbox{[}0, \doxylink{classeastl_1_1numeric__limits_a8192879def06192b5d8014b98be90fdb}{numeric\+\_\+limits$<$uint32\+\_\+t$>$\+::max()}\mbox{]}.

H2\+: a range-\/hashing function (in the terminology of Tavori and Dreizin). This is a function which takes the output of H1 and converts it to the range of \mbox{[}0, n\mbox{]}. Usually it merely takes the output of H1 and mods it to n.

H\+: a ranged hash function (Tavori and Dreizin). This is merely a class that combines the functionality of H1 and H2 together, possibly in some way that is somehow improved over H1 and H2 It is a binary function whose argument types are Key and size\+\_\+t and whose result type is \doxylink{eabase_8h_a435d1572bf3f880d55459d9805097f62}{uint32\+\_\+t}. Given arguments k and n, the return value is in the range \mbox{[}0, n). Default\+: h(k, n) = h2(h1(k), n). If H is anything other than the default, H1 and H2 are ignored, as H is thus overriding H1 and H2.

Rehash\+Policy\+: Policy class with three members, all of which govern the bucket count. n\+Bucket(n) returns a bucket count no smaller than n. Get\+Bucket\+Count(n) returns a bucket count appropriate for an element count of n. Get\+Rehash\+Required(n\+Bucket\+Count, n\+Element\+Count, n\+Element\+Add) determines whether, if the current bucket count is n\+Bucket and the current element count is n\+Element\+Count, we need to increase the bucket count. If so, returns pair(true, n), where n is the new bucket count. If not, returns pair(false, $<$anything$>$).

Currently it is hard-\/wired that the number of buckets never shrinks. Should we allow Rehash\+Policy to change that?

b\+Cache\+Hash\+Code\+: true if we store the value of the hash function along with the value. This is a time-\/space tradeoff. Storing it may improve lookup speed by reducing the number of times we need to call the Equal function.

b\+Mutable\+Iterators\+: true if \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_ab8c71d59d872293db64a74ce62e5c1ae}{hashtable\+::iterator} is a mutable iterator, false if iterator and \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_a849ca231be23a577007022b3f8c15558}{const\+\_\+iterator} are both const iterators. This is true for \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__map}{hash\+\_\+map} and \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__multimap}{hash\+\_\+multimap}, false for \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__set}{hash\+\_\+set} and \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__multiset}{hash\+\_\+multiset}.

b\+Unique\+Keys\+: true if the return value of hashtable\+::count(k) is always at most one, false if it may be an arbitrary number. This is true for \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__set}{hash\+\_\+set} and \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__map}{hash\+\_\+map} and is false for \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__multiset}{hash\+\_\+multiset} and \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__multimap}{hash\+\_\+multimap}.

Note\+: If you want to make a hashtable never increase its bucket usage, call set\+\_\+max\+\_\+load\+\_\+factor with a very high value such as 100000.\+f.

find\+\_\+as In order to support the ability to have a hashtable of strings but be able to do efficiently lookups via char pointers (i.\+e. so they aren\textquotesingle{}t converted to string objects), we provide the find\+\_\+as function. This function allows you to do a find with a key of a type other than the hashtable key type. See the find\+\_\+as function for more documentation on this.

find\+\_\+by\+\_\+hash In the interest of supporting fast operations wherever possible, we provide a find\+\_\+by\+\_\+hash function which finds a node using its hash code. This is useful for cases where the node\textquotesingle{}s hash is already known, allowing us to avoid a redundant hash operation in the normal find path.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classeastl_1_1hashtable_aef2992646778092aace2a36f6cb1c968} 
template$<$typename K, typename V, typename A, typename EK, typename Eq, typename H1, typename H2, typename H, typename RP, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} bC, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} bM, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} bU$>$ \\
template$<$typename U, typename UHash, typename Binary\+Predicate$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable}{hashtable}}$<$ K, V, A, EK, Eq, H1, H2, H, RP, bC, bM, bU $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_ab8c71d59d872293db64a74ce62e5c1ae}{\+::iterator}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable}{eastl\+::hashtable}}$<$ K, V, A, EK, Eq, H1, H2, H, RP, bC, bM, bU $>$\+::find\+\_\+as (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_ab71d9359ab4dbf7b609d9f5680e28843}{const}} U \&}]{u}{, }\item[{UHash}]{uhash}{, }\item[{Binary\+Predicate}]{predicate}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Implements a find whereby the user supplies a comparison of a different type than the hashtable \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hashtable_ad14dbaeeb2ca77ef6432bd19401c638d}{value\+\_\+type}. A useful case of this is one whereby you have a container of string objects but want to do searches via passing in char pointers. The problem is that without this kind of find, you need to do the expensive operation of converting the char pointer to a string so it can be used as the argument to the find function.

Example usage (namespaces omitted for brevity)\+: \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__set}{hash\+\_\+set$<$string$>$} hash\+Set; hash\+Set.\+find\+\_\+as("{}hello"{}); // Use default hash and compare.

Example usage (note that the predicate uses string as first type and char\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} as second)\+: \doxylink{classeastl_1_1hash__set}{hash\+\_\+set$<$string$>$} hash\+Set; hash\+Set.\+find\+\_\+as("{}hello"{}, hash$<$char\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}$>$(), equal\+\_\+to$<$$>$()); 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 35
